[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`handler_ber` fuzzing harness.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing with libFuzzer, the `handler_ber` entry point invoked the BER[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector on a crafted input. AddressSanitizer aborted execution, flagging a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-buffer overflow in `dissect_ber_GeneralString`.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Stack-based buffer overflow: a one-byte write past the boundary of a [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-allocated buffer.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Observations and Findings  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The overflow occurs at packet-ber.[0m[1;92mc:3194[0m[39m, inside `dissect_ber_GeneralString`. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The write goes beyond the bounds of the `name_string` array, which is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated in the caller stack frame of `try_dissect_unknown_ber` [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mpacket-ber.[0m[1;92mc:814[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The stack frame for `try_dissect_unknown_ber` contains `name_string` at [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffsets [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m160[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m240[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and the overflow happens at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m, indicating an underflow [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto the redzone.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
